          "body": "<h2>Plane crash in Colombia </h2> <p>A plane carrying a Brazilian football team flying to a cup final crashed in Colombia today, with 76 people reported dead. Initial reports suggested six of the 81 people aboard \u2013 72 passengers and nine crew members \u2013 had survived. According to Colombia\u2019s El Tiempo newspaper, there were at least 22 players from the Brazilian football club Chapecoense onboard, along with 22 football journalists from Brazil. The team was heading to Medell\u00edn to play in the Copa Sudamericana finals match against Atl\u00e9tico Nacional on Wednesday. The flight is believed to have taken off from S\u00e3o Paulo, Brazil, at 3.35pm local time and stopped off in Santa Cruz de la Sierra, Bolivia, before heading to Colombia. Medell\u00edn airport said in a statement that a plane travelling from Santa Cruz had declared an emergency because of an electrical failure and had crashed between the Colombian municipalities of La Ceja and La Uni\u00f3n. A unnamed 23rd player had reportedly intended to go on the trip but did not travel.</p> <p><a href=\"https://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/nov/29/plane-carrying-brazilian-footballers-team-chapecoense-crashes-en-route-to-medellin\">Brazilian team Chapecoense among those on board crashed plane</a></p>       <figure class=\"element element-video\" data-canonical-url=\"https://www.theguardian.com/world/video/2016/nov/29/plane-brazil-chapecoense-football-team-crash-colombia-video\"            data-short-url=\"https://gu.com/p/5dhpk\"                    data-show-ads=\"true\"            data-video-id=\"2926172\"            data-video-name=\"Plane carrying Brazil's Chapecoense football team crashes in Colombia \u2013\u00a0video report\"            data-video-provider=\"AP\"            > <video data-media-id=\"gu-video-583d408ce4b015a427f75b67\" class=\"gu-video\" controls=\"controls\" poster=\"\"> <source src=\"https://cdn.theguardian.tv/mainwebsite/2016/11/29/161129ColombiaUpdate2_desk.mp4\"/><source src=\"https://cdn.theguardian.tv/HLS/2016/11/29/161129ColombiaUpdate2.m3u8\"/><source src=\"https://cdn.theguardian.tv/webM/2016/11/29/161129ColombiaUpdate2_WebM.webm\"/> </video> <figcaption><a href=\"https://www.theguardian.com/world/video/2016/nov/29/plane-brazil-chapecoense-football-team-crash-colombia-video\">Plane carrying Brazil\u2019s Chapecoense football team crashes in Colombia \u2013 video report</a></figcaption> </figure>   <h2>Who are Chapecoense?</h2> <p>The Brazilian team onboard the plane was set to celebrate a historic week in its history. Chapecoense was travelling to Colombia to compete in its first continental final. The mood in the camp had been buoyant after the team \u2013 a relative outsider \u2013 had beaten several heavyweights to reach the final.</p> <p><a href=\"https://www.theguardian.com/football/2016/nov/29/chapecoense-brazilian-football-team-plane-crash-colombia\">Chapecoense: who are the Brazilian team on board the plane that crashed?</a></p> <h2>Support the Guardian\u2019s fearless journalism</h2> <p>Never has America needed <a href=\"http://click.mail.theguardian.com/?qs=459321946e415b12582921e8c24a8bd1742ea936a2899be565fa57f54568cd44\">fearless independent media more</a>. Help us hold the new president to account, sort fact from fiction, amplify underrepresented voices, and understand the forces behind this divisive election \u2013 and what happens next. Amid fears that there may have been foreign tampering with electronic voting systems, half a dozen academics and experts joined the suit to testify that recounting by hand would produce a \u201cmore correct result and change the outcome of the election\u201d, the suit said. </p> <p>The Green party presidential candidate has led a campaign, backed by crowdsourced fundraising, to have the votes in the crucial states of Wisconsin, Michigan, and Pennsylvania recounted. Her campaign has faced several roadblocks since she filed the first call for a recount in Wisconsin on Friday, as she may have missed the deadline for a recount in several counties in Pennsylvania and the state of Wisconsin is requesting $3.5m, more than the originally estimated $1m, by the end of Tuesday. </p> <p><a href=\"https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2016/nov/29/security-experts-join-jill-steins-election-changing-recount-campaign\">Security experts join Jill Stein\u2019s \u2018election changing\u2019 recount campaign</a></p>       <figure class=\"element element-video\" data-canonical-url=\"https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/video/2016/nov/25/jill-stein-calls-for-recount-in-order-to-verify-us-election-result-video\"            data-short-url=\"https://gu.com/p/5dxvh\"                    data-show-ads=\"true\"            data-video-id=\"2913830\"            data-video-name=\"Jill Stein calls for recount in order to verify US election result \u2013 video\"            data-video-provider=\"Facebook/Jill Stein\"            > <video data-media-id=\"gu-video-583887abe4b0cc60d3477172\" class=\"gu-video\" controls=\"controls\" poster=\"\"> <source src=\"https://cdn.theguardian.tv/mainwebsite/2016/11/25/161125jillstein2_desk.mp4\"/><source src=\"https://cdn.theguardian.tv/HLS/2016/11/25/161125jillstein2.m3u8\"/><source src=\"https://cdn.theguardian.tv/webM/2016/11/25/161125jillstein2_WebM.webm\"/> </video> <figcaption><a href=\"https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/video/2016/nov/25/jill-stein-calls-for-recount-in-order-to-verify-us-election-result-video\">Jill Stein calls for recount in order to verify US election result</a></figcaption> </figure>   <h2>Trump picks health secretary</h2> <p><a draggable=\"true\" href=\"https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/donaldtrump\">Donald Trump</a> has chosen a prominent critic of Obamacare as his secretary of health and human services, casting fresh doubt over the future of the Affordable Care Act. Congressman Tom Price of Georgia, an orthopedic surgeon who has long been a leading congressional voice in opposition to Barack Obama\u2019s healthcare reform legislation, was confirmed on Tuesday as the president-elect\u2019s pick. It came at the beginning of a day that Vice-President-elect Mike Pence told reporters would produce \u201ca number of very important announcements\u201d concerning the presidential transition.</p> <p><a href=\"https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2016/nov/28/tom-price-health-human-services-secretary-trump-administration\">Donald Trump selects Tom Price as secretary of health and human services</a><br /></p> <h2>Bannon\u2019s Hollywood days</h2> <p>John Patterson takes a look at the Hollywood career of Trump\u2019s chief strategist Steve Bannon \u2013 or Stephen K Bannon, as he\u2019s known on IMDb. Bannon, who has a record of promoting antisemitic, anti-Muslim and misogynistic content while overseeing the \u201calt-right\u201d website Breitbart News, made money through an early investment in Seinfeld, and later took to writing and producing his own films, including Hillary: The Movie and the Sarah Palin biopic The Undefeated. Bannon\u2019s \u201cmovies aim to give the illusion of authority and thoroughness, and they dig deep into the negatives on their enemies (Clinton Cash) and the positives on their idols (Palin biopic The Undefeated)\u201d, Patterson writes, \u201cwithout ever offering countervailing opinions or contrary evidence. No alternative opinion is wanted or sought. Only haters need apply.\u201d</p> <p><a href=\"https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2016/nov/29/steve-bannon-documentary-films-donald-trump\">For haters only: watching Steve Bannon\u2019s documentary films</a></p> <h2>Democrats \u2018must return to the left\u2019</h2> <p>The Democrats must abandon their centrist tendencies and return to the left if they are to win back the white working class, Thomas Frank argues. Frank says this election was a rebuke of centrist policies, which are predicated on the promise of victory, and implores Democrats to learn this lesson and pivot to the left. However, he has little hope that they will.</p> <p><a href=\"https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2016/nov/29/how-the-democrats-could-win-again-if-they-wanted\">How the Democrats could win again, if they wanted</a></p> <h2>In case you missed it</h2> <p>The newborn universe may have glowed with light beams moving much faster than they do today, according to a theory that overturns Einstein\u2019s century-old claim that the speed of light is a constant.</p> <p><a href=\"https://www.theguardian.com/science/2016/nov/28/theory-challenging-einsteins-view-on-speed-of-light-could-soon-be-tested\">Theory challenging Einstein\u2019s view on speed of light could soon be tested</a><br /></p>       <figure class=\"element element-video\" data-canonical-url=\"https://www.theguardian.com/science/video/2016/nov/29/was-einstein-wrong-physicists-challenge-speed-of-light-theory-video-explainer\"            data-short-url=\"https://gu.com/p/5dg92\"                    data-show-ads=\"true\"            data-video-id=\"2924993\"            data-video-name=\"Was Einstein wrong?
